id=\"emoji5_introduction\" class=\"col-md-4 col-md-offset-2\">\n            Notice that these are new emoji version <strong>Emoji 5.0</strong> or <strong>Unicode 10 Emoji</strong> that are planned for release in the Summer of 2017. But you can use it now by copying the emoji image (instead of just by clicking to copy the emoji code like other older emojis). Please <span class=\"instruct\">right click</span> on an emoji and choose <span class=\"instruct\">Copy Image</span> to copy it to the clipboard.
